Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: cherry\\ \tt RIGHT: lip gloss\\ \tt TOP: tulip\\ \tt BOTTOM: elephant\\ \tt CENTER: harps\\ \tt NORTHWEST: accordion\\ \tt NORTHEAST: banjo\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: evening gown\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: bronzer\\ \tt HERE: tiger\\ \tt THERE: spider\\ \tt NOWHERE: buttercup\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: jackfruit\\ \tt INSIDE: iodine\\ \tt OUTSIDE: toolbelt\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <one sentence>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <one sentence>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start.

	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 Answer is correct. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   } 
	 & & \\ 
 

    \theutterance \stepcounter{utterance}  

    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{\cellcolor[rgb]{0.95,0.95,0.95}{%
	\makecell[{{p{\linewidth}}}]{% 
	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 End probing 
	  } 
	   } 
	   } 
	 & & \\
